<!-- Script for Docked Sliver -->
<script>
$(function() {
  var $document = $(document);
  var $sliver = $('#ShippingSliverContainer');
  var sliverTop = $sliver.offset().top;
  $sliver.css({
    'top': 0,
    'z-index': 99, // top nav team select is 100, that still needs to show over this
    'padding-right' : '5px',
    'max-width': '100vw',
    'min-width': '1014px'
  });

  $(window).scroll(function() {
    var next = $document.scrollTop() > sliverTop ? "fixed" : "relative"
    if (next !== $sliver.css('position')) {
      $sliver.css('position', next);
    }
  }).scroll(); // trigger the event once at the beginning incase page reload happens when scrolled down

  //using reveal's opened event to make modal viewable when user is scrolled down the page
  //** ADD THIS LINE OF CODE WHEN USING REVEAL MODAL FOR TS&CS **
    $document.on('opened.fndtn.reveal', '[data-reveal]', function () {
      var $NFLModal = $(this);

      $NFLModal.css('position', 'fixed');
    });
});
</script>
<!-- END: Script for Docked Sliver -->

<script> /* global TCS, Image */
;(function (options) {
  /* ********* MAIN SETTINGS ********* */
  var lightboxImage = options.lightboxImage
  var lightboxLink = options.lightboxLink
  var lightboxCookie = options.lightboxCookie
  var lightboxCookieMinutes = options.lightboxCookieMinutes
  var bannerId = options.bannerId
  var excludePSIDs = options.excludePSIDs
  /* ********* MAIN SETTINGS ********* */

  // Determine if we should show the modal:

  // Only show the first interstitial
  if (window.hasShownInterstitial) {
    return
  }
  window.hasShownInterstitial = true

  // Don't show on checkout
  if (window.location.pathname.toLowerCase().indexOf('/checkout/') !== -1) {
    // don't show on checkout
    return
  }

  // Lightbox content
  var body = document.body
  // Create the overlay, add to body
  var overlay = document.createElement('div')
  overlay.setAttribute('id', 'lightboxOverlay')
  body.appendChild(overlay)

  // Create & add css
  var css = [
    // Base Overlay Styles
    'body {position: relative !important;}',
    '#lightboxModal { z-index: 10001; padding:0; position: fixed; left: 50%; top: 50%; margin-top: -300px; margin-left: -300px; display: none; }',
    '#lightboxCloseImg { width: 40px; height: 40px; position: absolute; top: -15px; right: -15px; z-index: 10002; }',
    '#lightboxModal .primary { border:0; outline: none; height: auto; width: 100%; margin: 0px auto; text-align: center; }',
    '#lightboxOverlay {position: fixed; top:0; left:0; width: 100%; height: 100%; background-color: #000; filter:alpha(opacity=75); -moz-opacity:0.75; -khtml-opacity: 0.75; opacity: 0.75; z-index: 10000; display: none; }',
    // Mobile Styles
    '@media(max-width: 1000px) {#lightboxModal { left: 10%; right: 10%; top: 10%; margin: 0px auto; text-align: right; }}'
  ].join('\n')
  var style = document.createElement('style')
  style.innerHTML = css
  body.insertBefore(style, body.firstChild)

  // Create modal, add to body
  var modal = document.createElement('div')
  // Please use this id so we can track the interstitial being shown
  modal.setAttribute('id', 'lightboxModal')
  modal.innerHTML = '<a href="' + lightboxLink + '" title="Shop the Sale"><img src="' + lightboxImage + '" alt="Sale" class="primary" /></a> <a id="lightboxSaleCloseLink" href="javascript:" title="Close"><img id="lightboxCloseImg" src="//fansedge.frgimages.com/partners/fanatics/madnessSaleX.png" alt="Close" /></a>'
  body.appendChild(modal)

  // Show the modal
  function show () {
    modal.style['display'] = overlay.style['display'] = 'block'
  }

  // Hide the modal
  function hide () {
    modal.style['display'] = overlay.style['display'] = 'none'
  }

  overlay.onclick = hide
  modal.lastChild.onclick = hide
  body.onkeyup = function (e) {
    if (e.keyCode === 27) {
      hide()
    }
  }

  // Close when clicking lightbox/content
  if (!lightboxLink) {
    modal.onclick = hide
  }

  // Show when clicking banner
  var banner = document.getElementById(bannerId)
  if (banner) {
    banner.onclick = show
  }

  // Set a cookie to hide the modal for x minutes
  var shouldShow = document.cookie.indexOf(lightboxCookie) === -1
  var expireDate = new Date()
  expireDate.setTime(expireDate.getTime() + (lightboxCookieMinutes * 60 * 1000))
  document.cookie = lightboxCookie + '=seen; expires=' + expireDate.toUTCString() + '; path=/'

  // Exclude from PSIDs
  var siteID = (window.Maxymiser && window.Maxymiser.PSID) ? window.Maxymiser.PSID : null
  if (siteID != null && excludePSIDs && excludePSIDs.replace(/\s/g, '').split(',').indexOf(parseInt(siteID, 10)) !== -1) {
    shouldShow = false
  }

  // Show now!
  // Don't show lightbox immediately if the cookie exists
  if (shouldShow) {
    // Wait for image to load before showing
    var img = new Image()
    img.onload = show
    img.src = lightboxImage
  }

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

function getCookie(name) {
    var cookie = document.cookie;
    var cookieNames = cookie.split(';');
    var cookieValue = '';
    if(name.indexOf('=') < 0){
       name = name + '=';
    }
    jQuery.each(cookieNames, function (i, item) {
        var trimmedItem = jQuery.trim(item).toLowerCase();
        var itemIndex = trimmedItem.indexOf(name);
	if (itemIndex >= 0){
           cookieValue = trimmedItem.substring(name.length,trimmedItem.length);
           return false;
	}
    });

    return cookieValue;
};
